  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9.35pt;text-align:left;"><span style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Pursuant to the requirements of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, the registrant has duly caused this report to be signed on its behalf by the undersigned hereunto duly authorized.</span></p>

  <title>EX-99.1</title>
 </head>
 <body style="margin: auto!important;padding: 8px;line-height: 1;">
  <div style="z-index:-3;min-height:0.5in;position:relative;"></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:14pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Runway Growth Finance Corp. Reports Third Quarter 2024 Financial Results</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Delivered Total and Net Investment Income of $36.7 million and $15.9 million, Respectively</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Investment Portfolio of $1.1 billion</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Conference Call Today, Tuesday, November 12, 2024, at 5:00 p.m. ET</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">MENLO PARK, Calif., November 12, 2024&#x2014;Runway Growth Finance Corp. (Nasdaq: RWAY) </font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">(&#x201c;Runway Growth&#x201d; or the &#x201c;Company&#x201d;),</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> a leading provider of flexible capital solutions to late- and growth-stage companies seeking an alternative to raising equity, today announced its financial results for the third quarter ended September 30, 2024.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Third Quarter 2024 Highlights</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:6.667%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:4pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.571084182443509%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Total investment income of $36.7 million </font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:6.667%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:4pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.571084182443509%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Net investment income of $15.9 million, or $0.41 per share</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:6.667%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:4pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.571084182443509%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Net asset value of $13.39 per share </font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:6.667%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:4pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.571084182443509%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Dollar-weighted annualized yield on debt investments of 15.9% </font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:6.667%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:4pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.571084182443509%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Two investments completed in new portfolio companies, four investments with existing portfolio companies, and one investment with our joint venture, representing $75.3 million in funded investments</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:6.667%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:4pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.571084182443509%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Aggregate proceeds of </font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">$75.0 million</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> in a principal prepayment, $10.0 million from an assignment to our joint venture, and $0.6 million from scheduled amortizations</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:6.667%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:4pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.571084182443509%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Repurchased 644,763 shares of the Company's common stock during the third quarter under previously authorized share repurchase program</font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Fourth Quarter 2024 Distributions</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:6.667%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:4pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.571084182443509%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Declared fourth quarter 2024 regular dividend of $0.40 per share</font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#x201c;Runway Growth delivered strong financial performance in the third quarter, reporting sequential net investment income growth and solid originations,&#x201d; said David Spreng, Founder and CEO of Runway Growth. &#x201c;Additionally, we funded seven investments during the quarter, expanding our high-quality portfolio of late and growth stage companies. Subsequent to quarter end, RWAY&#x2019;s investment adviser announced a business combination with BC Partners that will present the BDC with expanded origination opportunities, enhanced financing solutions, and continuity of leadership for years to come. As we near the end of 2024, we believe the Company is positioned to accelerate growth and drive long-term shareholder value.&#x201d;</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Third Quarter 2024 Operating Results</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Total investment income for the quarter ended September 30, 2024 was $36.7 million, compared to $43.8 million for the quarter ended September 30, 2023.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Net investment income for the quarter ended September 30, 2024 was $15.9 million, or $0.41 per share, compared to $22.0 million, or $0.54 per share, for the quarter ended September 30, 2023.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">The Company's dollar-weighted annualized yield on average debt investments for the quarter ended September 30, 2024 was 15.9%</font><font style="color:#231f20;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">. </font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">The Company calculates the yield on dollar-weighted debt investments for any period measured as (1) total investment-related income during the period divided by (2) the daily average of the fair value of debt investments, including investments on non-accrual status, outstanding during the period.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Total operating expenses for the quarter ended September 30, 2024 were $20.8 million, compared to $21.7 million for the quarter ended September 30, 2023.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Net realized gain (loss) on investments was zero for both quarters ended September 30, 2024 and September 30, 2023.</font></p>
  <div class="page-node-content"><div style="z-index:-3;flex-direction:column;display:flex;min-height:0.5in;justify-content:flex-end;position:relative;"></div></div>
  <hr style="margin-inline-start:auto;margin-inline-end:auto;page-break-after:always;">
  <div style="z-index:-3;min-height:0.5in;position:relative;"></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">For the quarter ended September 30, 2024, net change in unrealized gain on investments was $9.2 million, compared to a net change in unrealized loss on investments of $7.2 million for the comparable prior year period.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Portfolio and Investment Activity</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">As of September 30, 2024, Runway Growth&#x2019;s investment portfolio had an aggregate fair value of approximately $1.07 billion in 57 portfolio companies, and was comprised of approximately $1.00 billion in term loans, 98.6% of which are senior secured loans, and $62.2 million in warrants and other equity-related investments.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">During the third quarter of 2024, Runway Growth funded two investments in new portfolio companies and five investments in existing companies, representing $74.0 million in funded loans, net of upfront loan origination fees.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Total portfolio investment activity for the three and nine months ended September 30, 2024 was as follows:</font></p>

  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Net Asset Value</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">As of September 30, 2024, net asset value (&#x201c;NAV&#x201d;) per share was $13.39, compared to $14.08 as of September 30, 2023. Total net assets at the end of the third quarter was $507.4 million, down 11% from $570.5 million as of September 30, 2023.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">For the quarter ended September 30, 2024, net increase in net assets resulting from operations was $25.0 million, or $0.65 per share, compared to a net increase in net assets resulting from operations of $14.8 million, or $0.37 per share, for the quarter ended September 30, 2023.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Liquidity and Capital Resources</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">As of September 30, 2024, the Company had approximately $251.6 million in available liquidity, including unrestricted cash and cash equivalents of $3.6 million and $248.0 million in available borrowing capacity under the Company&#x2019;s credit facility, subject to existing terms, advance rates and regulatory and covenant requirements.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">The Company ended the quarter with a core leverage ratio of approximately 108%, compared to 110% for the quarter ended June 30, 2024.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Distributions</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">On November 5, 2024, the Company&#x2019;s board of directors declared a regular quarterly distribution of $0.40 per share for the fourth quarter of 2024, payable on December 2, 2024, to stockholders of record as of November 18, 2024.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>

  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Recent Developments</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">The Company evaluated events subsequent to </font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">September 30, 2024</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> through November 12, 2024, the date the consolidated financial statements were issued.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">On October 9, 2024, the Company received a full repayment of $8.0 million on its senior secured loan to Betterment Holdings, Inc.</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">On October 16, 2024, the Company sold its outstanding warrants for Dtex Systems, Inc. for proceeds of $1.9 million.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">On October 31, 2024, the Company received a partial repayment of $2.1 million on its senior secured loan to FiscalNote Holdings, Inc.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">On October 31, 2024, the Company received a full repayment of $18.5 million on its senior secured loans to Predactiv, Inc. (fka Sharethis, Inc.).</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">On October 31, 2024, the Company announced that Runway Growth Capital LLC (&#34;RGC&#34;) entered into an Agreement and Plan of Merger pursuant to which RGC Group Acquisition, LLC (the &#34;New Owner&#34;), a newly formed wholly owned subsidiary of BCP Special Opportunities Fund III, an affiliate of BC Partners Advisors L.P., will acquire RGC. The transaction will constitute a change of control of RGC, resulting in an assignment and subsequent termination of the Company's current investment advisory agreement with RGC (the &#34;Current Advisory Agreement&#34;). On October 29, 2024, the Board of Directors approved a proposed new investment advisory agreement (the &#34;New Advisory Agreement&#34;) by and between the Company and RGC, the terms of which are identical to the Current Advisory Agreement. On November 1, 2024, the Company filed with the SEC, a preliminary proxy statement relating to a special meeting of the Company's stockholders, currently planned to be held on December 13, 2024, at which the Company will seek stockholder approval of the New Advisory Agreement. If approved, the New Advisory Agreement will take effect following the closing of the transaction between RGC and the New Owner.</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">On November 5, 2024, the Board of Directors declared a regular distribution of $0.40 per share for stockholders of record as of November 18, 2024 payable on or before December 2, 2024.</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">From October 1, 2024 through November 11, 2024, the Company repurchased 528,305 shares under the Third Repurchase Program.</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Conference Call</font></p>

To participate in the conference call or webcast, participants should register online at the </font><font><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Runway Investor Relations website</font></font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">. The earnings call can also be accessed through the following links:</font></p>

  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">About Runway Growth Finance Corp.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Runway Growth is a growing specialty finance company focused on providing flexible capital solutions to late- and growth-stage companies seeking an alternative to raising equity. Runway Growth is a closed-end investment fund that has elected to be regulated as a business development company under the Investment Company Act of 1940, as amended. Runway Growth is externally managed by Runway Growth Capital LLC, an established registered investment advisor that was formed in 2015 and led by industry veteran David Spreng. For more information, please visit </font><font><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">www.runwaygrowth.com</font></font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Forward-Looking Statements</font></p>

All forward-looking statements speak only as of the date of this press release.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
